Mitchell Costello</Name>
< Text>
My wife Kendall and I took our cat here to be checked out. She keeps scratching her ear and we don't know why (and still don't know why). Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital, without actually seeing our cat prescribed a variety of medications and put her on a diet trial for 3 months and insisted she be in a cone for that duration of time. When asked to bring our cat in, they refused to examine our cat, claiming she was swiping at them, even though they also said they never took her out of the cat carrier to begin with (there was no way she could have gotten her paw through the holes in the cat carrier). They prescribed Gabapentin, an anticonvulsant medication claiming this would stop her from swiping at them in future visits and were gracious enough to charge us for it. Our cat was calm and fine going to and from the vet and is by nature and extremely friendly cat who sits in peoples laps when she meets them and we have never had this kind of issue with any other vet. We gave our cat this medication as prescribed, as well as daily dosages of Prednisolone (a steroid) and an anxiety medication and brought her back to the vet. They said she was still swiping at them (still having never taken her out of the cat carrier) and refused to examine our cat, told us to keep our cat in a cone and keep her on a diet trial for another 3 months while charging us for these visits and still having not examined or cat to see if this is even warranted. They graciously charged us for an examination both times without examining our cat and without providing any possible solutions other than long term medication, change of diet and continuous wearing of a cone. When told we would be soliciting a second opinion, they were very quick to give us our cat back without any pleasantries. I do not recommend this vet.< /Text>

<user_id>107739481524448874981<//user_id><username>Kay Thorson</username><date>1603129188314< /date>< rating>

<review>I went to a 24 hour veterinary hospital in Dublin, CA, for a year. I left when my "Rosita" was taken from me by a heartless, nonchalant, rude, non empathetic human being.
I thought I would never own another dog. Rosita's death shattered most of my heart. She was my "Emotional Support Therapy" dog and she loved me as much as I loved her.
After a few months of crying, sleeping and isolation, I decided to look online at the animal shelter in Dublin.
I was scanning pictures of the potential adoptees and my finger stopped. There she was, this cute, little imp of a face, with ears laid back. That was it!! She was staring back at me, with tiny, black eyes, yearning for her "forever" home.
I immediately called the shelter and asked if this sweet precious was still available for adoption. She was!!!
I jumped out of bed, got dressed and was there, faster than "greased lightening"!!
I was waiting in the yard, and one of the attendants opened the door. There she was, running on her leash like a banshee.
I picked her up and she curled up in my lap. I was a goner for this sweet girl. Turned out, she's a "Senior", just like me, with two, rather large, bald spots and a few, rotten teeth.
She received a vet check and I was told she is a "Chinese Crested" and ??? else.
It really was "love at first sight"!!!
I was on the hunt for a new doctor for "Miss Molly". We both decided that "Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital" would be our medical, grooming, nutritional facility.
The administrative employees, vet techs and veterinarians are ALL caring, knowledgeable, empathetic and kind. We've ALWAYS been treated like family and Miss Molly is always calm and collected, when we are there.
We are both very happy to recommend "Pleasanton Veterinary Hospital" for your animals' medical, grooming and nutritional needs.< /review>< Pics>

My name is Arian Eghbali, and I am the Chief Executive Officer of Enrich Financial.  There are many financial issues facing consumers today, such as estate planning, insurance, investments, and taxes, to name a few.  We are in the business of helping our clients meet all of their financial challenges. We do this by using a total wealth management approach. Each area is important individually, but managing them all collectively is one of the most important considerations in your overall financial success.

This Credit Repair Book focuses on only one aspect of our business.  Back in 2008, I decided that I wanted to focus more of my time and energy on assisting regular consumers, for whom this book has been prepared, to improve their credit health.  I realized that members of the upper middle class and wealthy citizens had adequate resources to hire large accounting, law, and financial consulting firms to handle their affairs, but that there was a shortage of companies working for the common, working man and woman.

That‚Äôs why I started a credit repair division of my company.  We have been successfully helping clients for years, by providing them with affordable plans and approaches to improve their credit. I‚Äôve tried my best to use plain, understandable words and to make this book user-friendly.   If you have the time, energy, and emotional wherewithal, you can perform many of these tasks yourself. <Time>1591536917591<//Time><rating>3</rating>< review>
For a Thai restaurant that isn't in Thai town or No Ho, this place is pretty good. They specialize in a lot of Northern Thai dishes, but I wasn't thrilled with my Khao Soi. Delicious, certainly. I ordered mine with crab and the crab was the best choice in my humble opinion. My big issues with my soup though was that it wasn't very hot when it came to me. I need my soups hot. Veggie egg rolls were good, don't forget to check in cause you will get them on the house if you drop $40. Coconut ice cream was too icy (not the way it should be) and the fried chicken was too dry. I will come back again though cause I am curious about the chicken over rice...</review>

<userid>113669553636359461479< /userid><name>Steve Cha</name><date>1620937382066</date><Rating>5< /Rating><text>Khao Soi Thai is a restaurant that is hard to see on the strip of Ventura Blvd, since it's tucked away in an outdoor shopping center. But don't miss it. It's a hidden gem. I say this because their food is really as delicious and as authentic as it gets, like something out of the Sherman Way Thai restaurants and Thai town in Hollywood. I think I've been here at least 5 times already, and I was always satisfied each time. What do I most recommend? Definitely, their Khao Soi noodles, which is a delicious coconut curry soup with noodles and chicken. Very good. I also loved their shrimp cake balls, their fried chicken, their pad kee mao, the crab fried rice, the pad gra pow over rice, the papaya salad. There's just too much to name. And you cannot miss out on the mango sticky rice dessert, when it is available in season. It's really one of the best I've had in a Thai restaurant or as street food.

So if you're in Studio City and looking for a great Thai restaurant, come to this place. I can safely say it's one of the best restaurants in Studio City, and the ambience is pretty cool here. Nice outdoor and indoor seating, and very reasonably priced. And Nicky was a great help!

I shot a Youtube video of my eating experience at Khao Soi Thai, which you can find on my Youtube channel, Rockstar Eater.< /text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPgK1KB8c16SMGAnkE1BaXkvSAJUO5jObpc6sqb=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNEqu7dwjQYmkGnFKbW7tnIiWAsx0uEzLaoDOjB=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNtM2hcs2uC9GCxf6GW978K41R_lF9psMzVzrIQ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< Response>

1542669049703</date>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
I came for the Khao Soi (can choose your protein and spice level) but I stayed for the crab fried rice, pad see ew, and spicy basil!

The Khao Soi is incredibly flavorful and the flavor is thick (it's a curry)but the soup is light and doesn't leave me feeling overly stuffed. The noodles are thick and LONG (I keep forgetting to ask for a knife - probably a faux paux) to cut the noodles... necessary when sharing the dish, which I highly recommend.

Crab Fried rice was delicious and the spicy basil (with pork) had me spooning in more before I even finished my first bite. I can't explain the flavors other than a must-try-for-yourself.

They have indoor as well as a cute outdoor, patio seating area- if the weather permits (ha- it's LA, aka always prime weather) and there's open seats I highly suggest sitting outside.
It's prime location on Ventura Blvd. but hidden in the shopping center where Peets coffee/Chin Chins is. Don't let the hidden gem aspect deter you, there's underground parking at the end of the alley.

I haven't tried anything here I didn't like and I'm determined to try the whole menu over time.

Along with serving delicious, authentic Thai cuisine,
Eric the owner, is the absolute best. Willing to talk, share and answer any questions or concerns.
I want to shout it from the top Runyon Canyon- Khao Soi Thai is your new favorite Thai place!< /text>

< review>
02/06/21
Sad to see that Pho Craft is gone. The owners were very nice, friendly and excellent chefs. I will miss their food and company. I wish them the best and hope they give it another try when we get past the current situation.

05/17/20
Update from the staff at Pho Craft:

We are happy to announce that we are open for take out orders beginning Monday, May 18th.

Our current Store Hours
Monday-Saturday: 11:00 am - 8:00 pm
Sunday: Closed

12/19
The House Special Pho was highly recommended and I can see why. The broth is rich and has a depth of flavor that reflects the use of cooking the soup with the bones for hours. We had a chance to speak to the chef who described how she makes the broth. No wonder it tastes so good.

Delicious food and friendly staff. Just a nice place to have a good meal. Prices are very reasonable.<//review>

So, this is not the typical place I would select if I just looked at the interior: If you didn't know, you would assume to be in a Dodgers fans' club house, with dark interior, multiple insignia, and endless screens. However, the food - typical by name - was in fact very good. What do you get: burgers - ha, no surprise! < Text>
In the ever present rivalry between BWW and Wingstop, the wing-off is won and lost in the execution. There are a few ways that the chicken here could be improved.

The chicken could definitely be juicier. The meat was dry and stringy. Then they can afford to put a bit more sauce on the wings. I don't know how much money they are saving from the reduced quantity of sauce, but they are losing revenue on people choosing their rivals.

The most mind numbing part is the service. No one is available to ask for the check, or refills, or asking questions. You have sit and wait... and wait... and wait. Not fun. I don't know why I came here...<//Text>
